I am, "Mr. Haoqi",
I am looking for "a story" and eating "a bowl of noodles".
‚ä¢‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚ä£
This is my first time staying in a Marriott executive apar**ent. I have stayed in many executive apar**ents of other hotel brands. Generally speaking, if the business trip lasts for a long time, the first choice will be a serviced apar**ent, which has a more "home" feeling. This time I was working in Yuzhong District and found it nearby.

üöïTransportation:
Airport, about 30 minutes,
Metro, Line 2 Jiaochangkou and Linjiangmen, two stations, about 200 meters away.
It is a 10-minute walk from Jiefangbei, Mountain City Trail, and Eighteen Stairs.
The entire Marriott building is named after it. Looking up, it's basically easy to find and you won't get lost. After a small downhill road, you will find the hotel entrance on the right hand side. There is a dedicated person at the door to guide the way, and every detail is in place.

üåøEnvironment:
For serviced apar**ents, the design of the basic lobby is mainly economical and not too big. In the Lobby on the 11th floor, there was basically no need to queue and check-in went smoothly. The overall design follows the general direction of Marriott and is a little more cozy.
I originally booked a double bed room, but was luckyly upgraded to a one-bedroom and one-living room at the front desk. I just had the opportunity to experience it and compare it with the previous Ascott.
Entering the door is the kitchen worktop and a living room that can accommodate 2-3 people. Entering the bedroom, placing a chair by the window is just right. It is indeed a good choice to have a book and a cup of coffee in the sun.
From the bed, to the dressing area, to the bathroom, the layout is reasonable and many facilities are new.

ü§µüèª‚ôÄÔ∏èService:
The service is still five-star standard and level. Much better than ordinary business hotels.

üç±Catering:
I just experienced the breakfast service. The shared Chinese restaurant is a pretty good environment. There are basic categories of breakfast, but there are few choices, and there is only one operating table around. In particular, Chongqing's most distinctive noodles taste very ordinary and fail to capture this highlight.

ü•ÉSmall comment:
Although it is my first time to stay here, from hardware to software, the experience is in place and the details are handled with care. This Marriott hotel is suitable for people traveling for business and tourism. If you choose it, you will basically avoid any pitfalls.
The only flaw is that there are relatively few breakfast categories and the quality needs to be improved.

Recommendation index: üåüüåüüåüüåüüåü

She has the nobility of spring and white snow, but does not reject the fireworks of the market at all. She is a lady who can control the hall and hold the kitchen. I like this city very much because it is lively and lively.
1. The apar**ent is within walking distance of the Jiefangbei business district, and many check-in spots, food and shopping spots are within walking distance. Some must-visit attractions in the city are not far away by taxi. The best thing is that there is a zebra crossing between the apar**ent and the downtown area. This is the perfect location to take a break from the bustle. The fly in the oin**ent is that there is a "wake-up service" for the demolition of the building at eight o'clock every day, and I don't know when the demolition and construction will be completed. The hotel is very close to the subway station and bus station. If you are used to getting off the elevator and driving directly to the parking lot at home, it will be great to experience public transportation in other places when staying at the Marriott. The nearby Light Rail Line 2 will reach Liziba Station at five or six stops. Take a look at the scene of a group of people holding up their mobile phones to take pictures of the subway passing through the building. You will find that the joy of life lies not only in the struggle in the business world, but also in the business world. It is certain seemingly simple, even straightforward happiness that will make you feel more relaxed. Why not temporarily take off your shrewd and reserved coat, "silly" take out your mobile phone, blend into that group of people, and look forward to the next subway train that passes through the building to appear in your lens?
2. The room type you live in is suitable for families, business trips, and even short-term rentals. It is a livable design with river and city views. Entering the large open room, the four functional areas of dining, kitchen, guest and book are integrated into one. It is equipped with a full set of Siemens washing machines, dryers, induction cookers, range hoods, refrigerators, microwave ovens, dishwashers and other electrical appliances. There are sofas, TVs, dining tables and Desks and other furniture, with pots and pans and air purifiers. Extending through the corridor, there are the master and guest bedrooms, each with a bathroom. The overall layout of the room is in a circular shape. Except for the second bedroom, all rooms have open windows, which is a bonus. The lighting sources in bedrooms, bathrooms and corridors are set scientifically. All hardware and software are relatively new.
3. The bedding continues Marriott's consistent comfort style and is suitable for sleeping. Among all the five-star chain brands I have experienced, I like Marriott‚Äôs bedding the most. Whether it is pillows, mattresses or quilts, they are flawless.
4. Talk about some commendable details: a full-length mirror for going out; a wardrobe, shoe cabinet and luggage rack with enough space; an extra refill of toilet paper and toilet paper will be placed for use; the kitchen is equipped with special kitchen paper; Sleeping spray, the old Marriott smell; the bedside table is also equipped with earplugs; the bathroom mirror is heated; large bottles of toiletries that cannot be canned, the old Marriott quality; bathrobes, towels, disposable items, slippers and slippers are provided according to the room type and number of guests. Bottled water, I have stayed here for many days, and I have not asked for replenishment once. Everything is enough, extra points; straight line (not circle line) blows the air.
5. What could be more perfect: the wash basin, makeup mirror and bathtub in the master bedroom bathroom are much higher in design than those in ordinary five-star hotels. The water pressure in the bathroom is not great, which is the biggest minus point. The lighting in the restaurant is dim.
6. Praise the concierge guy at B1. No matter which guy, he will help you press the elevator and pick up the luggage in advance. You can also get the elevator service from the concierge guy at twelve o'clock in the evening. There is a small table for takeout at the entrance of the hotel.
